caption: Can you spot the Eiffel Tower? 🗼
 ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀
 ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀
Another sunrise in my city. It’s (almost) impossible to get a picture without no one here during the day. It’s a very crowded roundabout and also a touristic place; Champs Élysées Avenue starts here as well. So on a sunny Sunday morning, I went to admire the beautiful morning colors. And it was very lovely ✨
 ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀
 ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀

It took 30 years to finish the Arc de Triomphe, and no wonder why: it's incredibly elaborate. Relief sculptures at the base of each of the four pillars show four victories and war scenes; the top of the arch has the names of major successes during the Revolutionary and Napoleonic periods. Less important victories can be found on the inside walls, plus the names of 558 generals. The underlined names are to show that the general died in battle. 🇫🇷

caption: #Paris #valeriegiscarddestaing dans mon objectif en 2018. Je garde de nos interviews son esprit vif, sa culture, sa distance avec le futile, son amour de la Grèce « en ce moment je relis Sophocle » m’avait-il dit « il faut relire les tragiques pour comprendre les méandres de la pensée des hommes ». Le président Giscard d’Estaing était un européen dans l’âme et dans les actes. C’est lui qui a oeuvré pour l’entrée de la Grèce dans la Communauté européenne en 1981, nous lui devons beaucoup. Il me parlait du président Caramanlis, de l’avion de la république française qu’il lui avait affrété à la chute des colonels « on ne fait pas jouer Platon en deuxième division » avait-il lancé à ceux qui s’opposaient à cet élargissement de la famille européenne. C’est aussi une part de notre enfance qui s’en va, le président d’avant les années quatre-vingt... il avait 94 ans. Je garde ce dernier sourire de notre dernière rencontre dans sa bibliothèque. Au revoir, monsieur le Président #ripvaleriegisgarddestaing #instanikos

Sono consapevole che il mondo che ho visto fino ad adesso viaggiando, nulla ha a che vedere con quello che vedrò. Prendo aerei da sempre, ma fino a questo momento si può dire che io sia solo e sempre andata in vacanza. Che sia per passione, che sia per svago, non mi sono mai confrontata - credo - con un viaggio vero. Uno di quelli che ti mette alla prova, in tutti i sensi.
"Sei pronta?"
"Come ti senti?"
"Sei felice?"
"Sei emozionata?"
"Non hai paura?"
"Ma perché stai andando lì? Sei pazza?!"

caption: Is this real life.. or is it a fairy tale?✨

One of the many gems of Annapolis is the historical William Paca house and gardens.

You wouldn’t expect this gorgeous two acre garden smack dab in the middle of the city.

For me, this has been a special place. I’ve worked here, had my rehearsal dinner here, picnicked here... it is such a gorgeous spot in my unique city🤍

This mansion was originally built between 1763 and 1765. In the 19th century, the home was converted into a hotel and then was later restored to its original design. 

What do you guys think? Would you want to visit?

likes: 179
caption: What is a physician associate and what do you we do?! 👩🏽‍⚕️
.
.
Physician associates are medically trained, generalist healthcare professionals, who work alongside doctors and provide medical care as an integral part of the multidisciplinary team. Physician associates are dependent practitioners working with a dedicated medical supervisor, but are able to work autonomously with appropriate support - FPA. 
.
.

PAs are trained via the medical model as opposed to the nursing model.

.
.

Our day to day roles include examining, investigations, management and diagnosis of different health conditions.🩺💉
.
:

We can work in any medical specialties- some of which include Cardiology, A&E, Obs&Gynae, Paediatrics and General Practice. 🌡🔬
.
.

Currently we cannot prescribe or request ionising radiation- although this might change in the neat future as PAs will be regulated by the GMC.
.
.

No we are not trying to take doctors or nursing jobs- we are an independent role and introduced in the NHS to reduce the workload. 🏥
.
.

If you are interested in applying to the Physician Associate course (a post graduate course)- then DM me for 1:1 coaching on application/interview help. 
.
.
.

caption: WHY Real Estate?⠀
⠀
My WHY is to help my generation, millennials, create environments so they can thrive mentally, physically & financially. ⠀
⠀
Real Estate happens to check ALL of the boxes. It started years ago when I read Rich Dad Poor Dad and it changed the way I thought about life, work and $. It’s well known that real estate builds wealth more consistently than other asset classes. ⠀
⠀
At the beginning of this year, quietly, I started the process of getting licensed, reading books, devouring podcasts, meeting other real estate professionals and shadowing as much as possible so I could accelerate the learning curve. ⠀
⠀
It’s crucial to surround yourself with like minded individuals that will push you, support you and challenging you to reach new heights. I found an incredible TEAM of real estate agents to work with in @livingnsandiego , and an incredible company that supports agents and is pushing the boundaries of the industry @compass . ⠀
⠀
People often ask me what happened to training… I will always love fitness. I loved @equinox . I’m eternally grateful for the relationships forged there, the experience I gained and then lessons I learned about life, business & more. ⠀
⠀
From working next to incredible people on a daily basis, to training some of the baddest human beings on the planet with the @theheroesproject Project and supporting rare cancer research with @cycleforsurvival . I will always stay connected to the PEOPLE. ⠀
⠀
In a similar fashion, Real Estate is a SERVICE INDUSTRY. Look at the press- we’re a LONG ways away from buying and selling properties online. There will always be HUMANS involved in a transaction. My goal is always to over deliver and SERVE my clients to the best of my abilities. Relationships, communication, integrity, work ethic and growth will always be my CORE VALUES. ⠀
⠀
This chapter of my life is just beginning, and I can’t wait to see where it goes. We’re already picking up steam and once the train gets going, there’s no looking back!

caption: One of the daily digests I subscribe to sent a “Top 20 December Do’s”… I decided to restructure, prioritize and narrow it down to my personal Top 10. ⠀
⠀
What are you doing in preparation for 2020?⠀
⠀
1. Reach out to your family and friends. They are the support system that really matters. Connect and re-connect.⠀
⠀
2. Get fit. Mental and physical health may be your best investment for the coming year. Schedule a daily workout, even if it's just a 20-minute walk.⠀
⠀
3. Did you have your annual physical/dentist? December could be a good month for health check-ups and maintenance.⠀
⠀
4.  Clean up and organize in preparation for 2020.⠀
⠀
5.  Install new systems for your workflow or refine those that already exist.⠀
⠀
6.  Structure your business plan for 2020. Think about this and write it down. Where did you succeed in 2019 and where could you improve? What opportunities may emerge in 2020? What new things could you be doing in 2020?⠀
⠀
7.  Look at your daily schedule and come up with some new daily tasks that you may not be doing already and install those in your calendar for all of 2020.⠀
⠀
8. Establish a daily reading list for 2020.⠀
⠀
9. Plan a vacation. Even if it's just a few days at home, enjoying the many attributes of your home and that which surrounds you. You need to turn off for a few days every now and then.⠀
⠀
10.  Meet with clients and colleagues for a coffee/lunch/drink/dinner.
